GT Equivalence Verification (PO2)
============================================================
GT: -alpha*v**c0 - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x - omega0**c4*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can match the GT expression:

**GT:** `-0.0892*v³ - 0.7253*v*(1 - x²) - 1.4474*x - 1.4474*x*exp(-|x|)`

Expanding: `-0.0892*v³ - 0.7253*v + 0.7253*v*x² - 1.4474*x - 1.4474*x*exp(-|x|)`

So the GT has these basis functions:
1. `v³` (coeff ≈ -0.0892)
2. `v` (coeff ≈ -0.7253)
3. `v*x²` (coeff ≈ 0.7253)
4. `x` (coeff ≈ -1.4474)
5. `x*exp(-|x|)` (coeff ≈ -1.4474)

The key challenge is matching `x*exp(-|x|)`. No candidate has an explicit `exp` term. So candidates must approximate `x*exp(-|x|)` using their available basis functions, which would NOT be exact equivalence.

Let me check if any candidate structure could exactly represent `x*exp(-|x|)`.

**Candidates with `x/(c*x² + 1)` type terms** (12, 19-31, 50): The function `x/(cx²+1)` is a rational function - it cannot exactly equal `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x. These are approximations only.

**Candidates with polynomial-only extra terms** (like x⁵, x⁷, x⁹): Polynomials cannot exactly represent `x*exp(-|x|)` - Taylor series of exp(-|x|) has infinitely many terms, and |x| introduces non-analyticity.

**Candidates with `x^c` terms** (where c is a free constant): `x^c` for non-integer c involves |x|^c * sign behavior, but this is a power function, not exponential. It cannot match `x*exp(-|x|)`.

**Candidates with `x*|x|` terms**: `x*|x| = x²*sign(x) = |x|*x`. This is not `x*exp(-|x|)`.

Let me verify: Can ANY combination of the basis functions present in these candidates (polynomials in x, v, x*|x|, x^c, x/(cx²+1), etc.) exactly equal `x*exp(-|x|)`? 

No. `x*exp(-|x|)` is a transcendental function that cannot be expressed as any finite combination of polynomials, `x*|x|`, power functions `x^c`, or rational functions `x/(cx²+1)`. These are fundamentally different function classes.

Since every candidate lacks an exponential term and none can exactly reproduce `x*exp(-|x|)`, none can be exactly equivalent to the GT.

Let me verify each candidate systematically - all candidates contain combinations of: `x^n`, `v`, `v*x²`, `v³`, `x*|x|`, `x^c`, `x/(cx²+1)`, and similar terms. None contain `exp(...)`. Therefore, by the linear independence of exponential and polynomial/rational/power basis functions, none can match.

Candidate 1-50 verdict: All [NO MATCH] because none can produce the `x*exp(-|x|)` term.
